00079     static uintptr_t vtableindexof(T memfuncptr);
00080 
00081     template <typename T>
00082     static uintptr_t adjustmentof(T memfuncptr);
00083 
00084     template <typename cls>
00085     static cls* generate_instance();
00086 
00087     template <typename cls>
00088     static cls* get_instance();
00089 
00090 
00091 
00092 
00093 
00094 
00095     static uintptr_t follow_thunk_function(uintptr_t address) noexcept
00096     {
00097       return address;
00098     }
00099 
00100     static bool is_virtual_impl(void* address) noexcept;
00101 
00102   };
00103 
00104   /*
00105    * TEMPLATE DEFINITIONS (ignore them)
00106    */
00107   template <utils::member_function_type  T >
00108   bool addresser::is_virtual(T memfuncptr)
00109   {
00110 
00111 
00112 
00113 
00114 
00115 
00116     return is_virtual_impl(reinterpret_cast<void*>(&memfuncptr));
00117   }
00118 
00119   template <utils::member_function_type  T >
00120   uintptr_t addresser::address_of(T memfuncptr)
00121   {
00122     if (is_virtual(memfuncptr))
00123       return address_of_virtual(memfuncptr);
00124     return address_of_regular(memfuncptr);
00125   }
00126 
00127   template <utils::member_function_type  T >
00128   uintptr_t addresser::address_of_virtual(T memfuncptr)
00129   {
00130     typedef utils::fn_class_t<T> cls;
00131 
00132     cls* inst = get_instance<cls>();
00133     if (!inst)
00134       return 0;
00135 
00136     uintptr_t vtable_index = vtableindexof(memfuncptr);
00137     uintptr_t adjustment   = adjustmentof(memfuncptr);
00138     uintptr_t address      = *reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t*>(
00139         *reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t*>(reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(inst) +
00140                                       adjustment) +
00141         vtable_index);
00142     return follow_thunk_function(address);
00143   }
00144 
00145   template <utils::member_function_type  T >
00146   uintptr_t addresser::address_of_regular(T memfuncptr)
00147   {
00148     return follow_thunk_function(*reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t*>(&memfuncptr));
00149   }
00150 
00151   template <typename T>
00152   uintptr_t addresser::vtableindexof(T memfuncptr)
00153   {
00154     typedef utils::fn_class_t<T> cls;
00155     typedef uintptr_t            (cls::*method_t)();
00156     return (reinterpret_cast<cls*>(instance())
00157                 ->*reinterpret_cast<method_t>(memfuncptr))();
00158   }
00159 
00160   template <typename T>
00161   uintptr_t addresser::adjustmentof(T memfuncptr)
00162   {
00163     if constexpr (sizeof(T) == sizeof(uintptr_t))
00164       return 0;
00165     else
00166     {
00167       uintptr_t adjustment = *(reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t*>(&memfuncptr) + 1);
00168       if (adjustment & 1)
00169         adjustment >>= 1;
00170       return adjustment;
00171     }
00172   }
00173 
00174   template <typename cls>
00175   cls* addresser::generate_instance()
00176   {
00177     if constexpr (has_instanceptrof<cls>)
00178       return instanceptrof<cls>{}();
00179     else if constexpr (std::is_abstract_v<cls> ||
00180                        !std::is_move_constructible_v<cls>)
00181       return nullptr;
00182     else
00183     {
00184       std::byte memoryblock[sizeof(cls)]{};
00185       return new cls(std::move(*reinterpret_cast<cls*>(memoryblock)));
00186     }
00187   }
00188 
00189   template <typename cls>
00190   cls* addresser::get_instance()
00191   {
00192     static cls* cache = generate_instance<cls>();
00193     return cache;
00194   }
00195 } // namespace alterhook

00029    * @brief A pure virtual function which at run-time tries to collect as much

00032    * of @ref alterhook::exceptions::alterhook_exception are meant to override

00494   class hook_chain::iterator
00495   {
00496   public:
00497 
00498     typedef std::forward_iterator_tag iterator_concept;
00499 
00500     typedef std::forward_iterator_tag iterator_category;
00501     typedef hook                      value_type;
00502     typedef ptrdiff_t                 difference_type;
00503     typedef hook*                     pointer;
00504     typedef hook&                     reference;
00505 
00506     iterator() noexcept = default;
00507 
00508     reference operator*() const noexcept { return *itrs[enabled]; }
00509 
00510     pointer operator->() const noexcept { return itrs[enabled].operator->(); }
00511 
00512     iterator& operator++() noexcept;
00513     iterator  operator++(int) noexcept;
00514 
00515     bool operator==(const iterator& other) const noexcept
00516     {
00517       return enabled == other.enabled && itrs[enabled] == other.itrs[enabled];
00518     }
00519 
00520     bool operator!=(const iterator& other) const noexcept
00521     {
00522       return enabled != other.enabled || itrs[enabled] != other.itrs[enabled];
00523     }
00524 
00525     operator list_iterator() const noexcept { return itrs[enabled]; }
00526 
00527     operator const_list_iterator() const noexcept { return itrs[enabled]; }
00528 
00529   private:
00530     friend class hook_chain;
00531     std::array<list_iterator, 2> itrs{};
00532     bool                         enabled = false;
00533 
00534     explicit iterator(list_iterator ditr, list_iterator eitr,
00535                       bool enabled) noexcept
00536         : itrs({ ditr, eitr }), enabled(enabled)
00537     {
00538     }
00539   };

00587   /*
00588    * TEMPLATE DEFINITIONS
00589    */
00590   template <typename dtr, typename orig, typename... types, typename>
00591   hook_chain::hook_chain(std::byte* target, dtr&& detour, orig& original,
00592                          types&&... rest)
00593       : trampoline(target)
00594   {
00595     init_chain(utils::make_index_sequence_with_step<sizeof...(types) + 2, 2>(),
00596                utils::make_index_sequence_with_step<sizeof...(types) + 2, 3>(),
00597                std::forward_as_tuple(std::forward<dtr>(detour), original,
00598                                      std::forward<types>(rest)...));
00599   }
00600 
00601   template <typename trg, typename dtr, typename orig, typename... types,
00602             typename>
00603   hook_chain::hook_chain(trg&& target, dtr&& detour, orig& original,
00604                          types&&... rest)
00605       : hook_chain(get_target_address(std::forward<trg>(target)),
00606                    std::forward<dtr>(detour), original,
00607                    std::forward<types>(rest)...)
00608   {
00609     helpers::assert_valid_target_and_detours<trg>(
00610         helpers::extract_detour_sequence_t<dtr, orig, types...>());
00611   }
00612 
00613   template <typename pair, typename... types, typename>
00614   hook_chain::hook_chain(std::byte* target, pair&& first, types&&... rest)
00615       : trampoline(target)
00616   {
00617     init_chain(
00618         std::make_index_sequence<sizeof...(types)>(),
00619         std::pair(
00620             std::forward_as_tuple(
00621                 std::forward<
00622                     std::tuple_element_t<0, utils::remove_cvref_t<pair>>>(
00623                     std::get<0>(first)),
00624                 std::forward<
00625                     std::tuple_element_t<0, utils::remove_cvref_t<types>>>(
00626                     std::get<0>(rest))...),
00627             std::forward_as_tuple(
00628                 std::forward<
00629                     std::tuple_element_t<1, utils::remove_cvref_t<pair>>>(
00630                     std::get<1>(first)),
00631                 std::forward<
00632                     std::tuple_element_t<1, utils::remove_cvref_t<types>>>(
00633                     std::get<1>(rest))...)));
00634   }
00635 
00636   template <typename trg, typename pair, typename... types, typename>
00637   hook_chain::hook_chain(trg&& target, pair&& first, types&&... rest)
00638       : hook_chain(get_target_address(std::forward<trg>(target)),
00639                    std::forward<pair>(first), std::forward<types>(rest)...)
00640   {
00641     helpers::assert_valid_target_and_detours<trg>(
00642         helpers::extract_detour_sequence_from_tuples_t<pair, types...>());
00643   }
00644 
00645   template <typename orig, typename>
00646   hook_chain::hook_chain(const alterhook::hook& other, orig& original)
00647       : trampoline(other)
00648   {
00649     memcpy(backup.data(), other.backup.data(), backup.size());
00650     ((void)0);
00651     list_iterator itr = disabled.emplace(disabled.end());
00652     itr->init(*this, itr, other.pdetour,
00653                ptrampoline.get() , original, false);
00654   }
00655 
00656   template <typename detour_t, typename original_t, size_t... d_indexes,
00657             size_t... o_indexes, typename... types>
00658   void hook_chain::init_chain(std::index_sequence<d_indexes...>,
00659                               std::index_sequence<o_indexes...>,
00660                               std::tuple<detour_t, original_t, types...>&& args)
00661   {
00662     typedef utils::type_sequence<detour_t, original_t, types...> seq;
00663     init_chain(std::make_index_sequence<sizeof...(d_indexes)>(),
00664                std::pair(std::forward_as_tuple(
00665                              std::forward<detour_t>(std::get<0>(args)),
00666                              std::forward<utils::type_at_t<d_indexes, seq>>(
00667                                  std::get<d_indexes>(args))...),
00668                          std::forward_as_tuple(
00669                              std::forward<original_t>(std::get<1>(args)),
00670                              std::forward<utils::type_at_t<o_indexes, seq>>(
00671                                  std::get<o_indexes>(args))...)));
00672   }
00673 
00674   template <typename dfirst, typename... detours, typename ofirst,
00675             typename... originals, size_t... indexes>
00676   void
00677       hook_chain::init_chain(std::index_sequence<indexes...>,
00678                              std::pair<std::tuple<dfirst, detours...>,
00679                                        std::tuple<ofirst, originals...>>&& args)
00680   {
00681     helpers::assert_valid_detour_and_original_pairs(
00682         utils::type_sequence<dfirst, detours...>(),
00683         utils::type_sequence<ofirst, originals...>());
00684 
00685     ((void)0);
00686     do   {   if (patch_above)   memcpy(backup.data(),   ptarget -   ::alterhook::detail::constants::patch_above_target_offset,   ::alterhook::detail::constants::patch_above_backup_size);   else   memcpy(backup.data(), ptarget,   ::alterhook::detail::constants::backup_size);   } while (false);
00687     hook& fentry = enabled.emplace_back();
00688     fentry.init(
00689         *this, enabled.begin(),
00690         get_target_address(std::forward<dfirst>(std::get<0>(args.first))),
00691          ptrampoline.get() , std::get<0>(args.second),
00692         true);
00693     starts_enabled = true;
00694 
00695     if constexpr (sizeof...(detours) > 0)
00696     {
00697       list_iterator    iter    = enabled.begin();
00698       hook*            entry   = &fentry;
00699       const std::byte* pdetour = entry->pdetour;
00700       ((entry = &enabled.emplace_back(),
00701         entry->init(*this, ++iter,
00702                     get_target_address(std::forward<detours>(
00703                         std::get<indexes + 1>(args.first))),
00704                     pdetour, std::get<indexes + 1>(args.second), true),
00705         pdetour = entry->pdetour),
00706        ...);
00707     }
00708     init_chain();
00709   }
00710 
00711   template <typename detour_t, typename original_t, size_t... d_indexes,
00712             size_t... o_indexes, typename... types>
00713   void
00714       hook_chain::append_impl(transfer to, std::index_sequence<d_indexes...>,
00715                               std::index_sequence<o_indexes...>,
00716                               std::tuple<detour_t, original_t, types...>&& args)
00717   {
00718     typedef utils::type_sequence<detour_t, original_t, types...> seq;
00719     append_impl(to, std::make_index_sequence<sizeof...(d_indexes)>(),
00720                 std::pair(std::forward_as_tuple(
00721                               std::forward<detour_t>(std::get<0>(args)),
00722                               std::forward<utils::type_at_t<d_indexes, seq>>(
00723                                   std::get<d_indexes>(args))...),
00724                           std::forward_as_tuple(
00725                               std::forward<original_t>(std::get<1>(args)),
00726                               std::forward<utils::type_at_t<o_indexes, seq>>(
00727                                   std::get<o_indexes>(args))...)));
00728   }
00729 
00730   template <typename dfirst, typename... detours, typename ofirst,
00731             typename... originals, size_t... indexes>
00732   void hook_chain::append_impl(
00733       transfer to, std::index_sequence<indexes...>,
00734       std::pair<std::tuple<dfirst, detours...>,
00735                 std::tuple<ofirst, originals...>>&& args)
00736   {
00737     helpers::assert_valid_detour_and_original_pairs(
00738         utils::type_sequence<dfirst, detours...>(),
00739         utils::type_sequence<ofirst, originals...>());
00740     auto [trg, other] = to == transfer::enabled ? std::tie(enabled, disabled)
00741                                                 : std::tie(disabled, enabled);
00742     hook&         first_entry = trg.emplace_back();
00743     list_iterator itr         = std::prev(trg.end());
00744     list_iterator itrcurrent  = itr;
00745     size_t        count       = 1;
00746 
00747     try
00748     {
00749       if (to == transfer::enabled)
00750       {
00751         ((void)0);
00752         const std::byte* original =
00753             itr == enabled.begin()
00754                 ?  ptrampoline.get() 
00755                 : std::prev(itr)->pdetour;
00756         hook* entry = nullptr;
00757         first_entry.init(
00758             *this, itr,
00759             get_target_address(std::forward<dfirst>(std::get<0>(args.first))),
00760             original, std::get<0>(args.second), true);
00761         original = first_entry.pdetour;
00762 
00763         ((entry = &enabled.emplace_back(),
00764           entry->init(*this, ++itrcurrent,
00765                       get_target_address(std::forward<detours>(
00766                           std::get<indexes + 1>(args.first))),
00767                       original, std::get<indexes + 1>(args.second), true),
00768           original = entry->pdetour, ++count),
00769          ...);
00770         join_last_unchecked(count);
00771       }
00772       else
00773       {
00774         hook* entry = nullptr;
00775         first_entry.init(
00776             *this, itr,
00777             get_target_address(std::forward<dfirst>(std::get<0>(args.first))),
00778             std::get<0>(args.second));
00779 
00780         ((entry = &disabled.emplace_back(),
00781           entry->init(*this, ++itrcurrent,
00782                       get_target_address(std::forward<detours>(
00783                           std::get<indexes + 1>(args.first))),
00784                       std::get<indexes + 1>(args.second)),
00785           ++count),
00786          ...);
00787       }
00788     }
00789     catch (...)
00790     {
00791       trg.resize(trg.size() - count);
00792       throw;
00793     }
00794 
00795     bool touch_back = false;
00796     if (itr == trg.begin())
00797     {
00798       if (other.empty())
00799         starts_enabled = static_cast<bool>(to);
00800       else
00801         touch_back = true;
00802     }
00803     else if (std::prev(itr)->has_other)
00804       touch_back = true;
00805 
00806     if (!touch_back)
00807       return;
00808     hook& otherback     = other.back();
00809     otherback.has_other = true;
00810     otherback.other     = itr;
00811   }
00812 
00813   template <typename orig, typename>
00814   void hook_chain::hook::init(hook_chain& chain, list_iterator curr,
00815                               const std::byte* detour,
00816                               const std::byte* original, orig& origref,
00817                               bool should_enable)
00818   {
00819     new (&origbuff) helpers::original_wrapper(origref);
00820     pchain    = &chain;
00821     current   = curr;
00822     pdetour   = detour;
00823     poriginal = original;
00824     enabled   = should_enable;
00825     origwrap  = std::launder(reinterpret_cast<helpers::original*>(&origbuff));
00826     origref   = function_cast<orig>(original);
00827   }
00828 
00829   template <typename orig, typename>
00830   void hook_chain::hook::init(hook_chain& chain, list_iterator curr,
00831                               const std::byte* detour, orig& origref)
00832   {
00833     new (&origbuff) helpers::original_wrapper(origref);
00834     pchain   = &chain;
00835     current  = curr;
00836     pdetour  = detour;
00837     origwrap = std::launder(reinterpret_cast<helpers::original*>(&origbuff));
00838     origref  = nullptr;
00839   }
00840 
00841   template <typename orig, typename>
00842   void hook_chain::hook::set_original(orig& original)
00843   {
00844     if (origwrap->contains_ref(original))
00845       return;
00846     helpers::orig_buff_t tmp{};
00847     new (&tmp) helpers::original_wrapper(original);
00848     set_original(tmp);
00849   }
00850 
00851   template <typename dtr, typename orig, typename>
00852   hook_chain::hook& hook_chain::insert(list_iterator position, dtr&& detour,
00853                                        orig& original, include trg)
00854   {
00855     helpers::assert_valid_detour_original_pair<dtr, orig>();
00856     
00857 assert(((void) "hook_chain::insert: base cannot be the both flag" ,  trg != include::both ));
00858     helpers::orig_buff_t buffer{};
00859     new (&buffer) helpers::original_wrapper(original);
00860     return insert_impl(position, get_target_address(std::forward<dtr>(detour)),
00861                        buffer, trg);
00862   }
00863 
00864   template <typename dtr, typename orig, typename>
00865   hook_chain::hook& hook_chain::insert(iterator position, dtr&& detour,
00866                                        orig& original)
00867   {
00868     return insert(static_cast<list_iterator>(position),
00869                   std::forward<dtr>(detour), original,
00870                   position.enabled ? include::enabled : include::disabled);
00871   }
00872 
00873   template <typename dtr, typename orig, typename... types, typename>
00874   void hook_chain::append(transfer to, dtr&& detour, orig& original,
00875                           types&&... rest)
00876   {
00877     if constexpr (sizeof...(rest) == 0)
00878       push_back(std::forward<dtr>(detour), original, static_cast<bool>(to));
00879     else
00880       append_impl(
00881           to, utils::make_index_sequence_with_step<sizeof...(rest) + 2, 2>(),
00882           utils::make_index_sequence_with_step<sizeof...(rest) + 2, 3>(),
00883           std::forward_as_tuple(std::forward<dtr>(detour), original,
00884                                 std::forward<types>(rest)...));
00885   }
00886 
00887   template <typename dtr, typename orig, typename... types, typename>
00888   void hook_chain::append(dtr&& detour, orig& original, types&&... rest)
00889   {
00890     append(transfer::enabled, std::forward<dtr>(detour), original,
00891            std::forward<types>(rest)...);
00892   }
00893 
00894   template <typename pair, typename... types, typename>
00895   void hook_chain::append(transfer to, pair&& first, types&&... rest)
00896   {
00897     if constexpr (sizeof...(rest) == 0)
00898       push_back(
00899           std::forward<std::tuple_element_t<0, utils::remove_cvref_t<pair>>>(
00900               std::get<0>(first)),
00901           std::forward<std::tuple_element_t<1, utils::remove_cvref_t<pair>>>(
00902               std::get<1>(first)),
00903           static_cast<bool>(to));
00904     else
00905       append_impl(
00906           to, std::make_index_sequence<sizeof...(rest)>(),
00907           std::pair(
00908               std::forward_as_tuple(
00909                   std::forward<
00910                       std::tuple_element_t<0, utils::remove_cvref_t<pair>>>(
00911                       std::get<0>(first)),
00912                   std::forward<
00913                       std::tuple_element_t<0, utils::remove_cvref_t<types>>>(
00914                       std::get<0>(rest))...),
00915               std::forward_as_tuple(
00916                   std::forward<
00917                       std::tuple_element_t<1, utils::remove_cvref_t<pair>>>(
00918                       std::get<1>(first)),
00919                   std::forward<
00920                       std::tuple_element_t<1, utils::remove_cvref_t<types>>>(
00921                       std::get<1>(rest))...)));
00922   }
00923 
00924   template <typename pair, typename... types, typename>
00925   void hook_chain::append(pair&& first, types&&... rest)
00926   {
00927     append(transfer::enabled, std::forward<pair>(first),
00928            std::forward<types>(rest)...);
00929   }
00930 
00931   template <typename dtr, typename orig, typename>
00932   void hook_chain::push_back(dtr&& detour, orig& original, bool enable_hook)
00933   {
00934     helpers::orig_buff_t buffer{};
00935     new (&buffer) helpers::original_wrapper(original);
00936     push_back_impl(get_target_address(std::forward<dtr>(detour)), buffer,
00937                    enable_hook);
00938   }
00939 
00940   template <typename dtr, typename orig, typename>
00941   void hook_chain::push_front(dtr&& detour, orig& original, bool enable_hook)
00942   {
00943     helpers::orig_buff_t buffer{};
00944     new (&buffer) helpers::original_wrapper(original);
00945     push_front_impl(get_target_address(std::forward<dtr>(detour)), buffer,
00946                     enable_hook);
00947   }
00948 
00949   template <typename itr>
00950   void hook_chain::append_items(itr first, itr last, transfer trg)
00951   {
00952     if (first == last)
00953       return;
00954     auto [to, other] = trg == transfer::enabled ? std::tie(enabled, disabled)
00955                                                 : std::tie(disabled, enabled);
00956     hook&         first_entry = to.emplace_back();
00957     size_t        count       = 1;
00958     list_iterator hitr        = std::prev(to.end());
00959     list_iterator hitrcurrent = hitr;
00960 
00961     try
00962     {
00963       if (trg == transfer::enabled)
00964       {
00965         ((void)0);
00966         const std::byte* original =
00967             enabled.empty() ?  ptrampoline.get() 
00968                             : std::prev(hitr)->pdetour;
00969         hook* entry = nullptr;
00970         first_entry.init(*this, hitr, first->pdetour, original,
00971                          first->origbuff);
00972         original = first_entry.pdetour;
00973         ++first;
00974 
00975         for (; first != last; ++first, ++count, original = entry->pdetour)
00976         {
00977           entry = &enabled.emplace_back();
00978           entry->init(*this, ++hitrcurrent, first->pdetour, original,
00979                       first->origbuff);
00980         }
00981         join_last_unchecked(count);
00982       }
00983       else
00984       {
00985         first_entry.init(*this, hitrcurrent, first->pdetour, first->origbuff);
00986         ++first;
00987 
00988         for (; first != last; ++first, ++count)
00989           disabled.emplace_back().init(*this, ++hitrcurrent, first->pdetour,
00990                                        first->origbuff);
00991       }
00992     }
00993     catch (...)
00994     {
00995       to.resize(to.size() - count);
00996       throw;
00997     }
00998 
00999     bool touch_back = false;
01000     if (hitr == to.begin())
01001     {
01002       if (other.empty())
01003         starts_enabled = static_cast<bool>(trg);
01004       else
01005         touch_back = true;
01006     }
01007     else if (std::prev(hitr)->has_other)
01008       touch_back = true;
01009 
01010     if (!touch_back)
01011       return;
01012     hook& otherback     = other.back();
01013     otherback.has_other = true;
01014     otherback.other     = hitr;
01015   }
01016 
01017   template <typename dtr, typename orig>
01018   typename hook_chain::hook hook_chain::hook_from(dtr&& detour, orig& original)
01019   {
01020     hook h{};
01021     h.pdetour = get_target_address(std::forward<dtr>(detour));
01022     new (&h.origbuff) helpers::original_wrapper(original);
01023     return h;
01024   }

01026   /*
01027    * NON-TEMPLATE DEFINITIONS
01028    */
01029   inline hook_chain::hook_chain(std::byte* target) : trampoline(target)
01030   {
01031     do   {   if (patch_above)   memcpy(backup.data(),   ptarget -   ::alterhook::detail::constants::patch_above_target_offset,   ::alterhook::detail::constants::patch_above_backup_size);   else   memcpy(backup.data(), ptarget,   ::alterhook::detail::constants::backup_size);   } while (false);
01032   }

01035   {
01036     iterator next = std::next(position);
01037     erase(static_cast<list_iterator>(position));
01038     return next;
01039   }

01041   inline void hook_chain::merge(hook_chain& other, bool at_back)
01042   {
01043     iterator where = at_back ? end() : begin();
01044     splice(where, other, other.begin(), other.end());
01045   }

01130   inline typename hook_chain::iterator hook_chain::begin() noexcept
01131   {

01136   {

01138                     disabled.empty() ? starts_enabled
01139                                      : disabled.back().has_other);
01140   }

01150                           disabled.empty() ? starts_enabled

01194   inline void hook_chain::assert_len(size_t n) const
01195   {
01196     (void)n;
01197     
01198 
01199 assert(((void) "hook_chain::operator[]: element at index specified is out of range" ,  n < size() ));
01200   }
01201 
01202   inline void hook_chain::verify_len(size_t n) const
01203   {
01204     if (n < size())
01205       return;
01206     std::stringstream stream{};
01207     stream << "Element at index " << n
01208            << " of the hook_chain instance is out of range because: n >= "
01209               "size() <=> "
01210            << n << " >= " << size();
01211     throw(std::out_of_range(stream.str()));
01212   }
01213 
01214   inline typename hook_chain::reference
01215       hook_chain::operator[](size_t n) noexcept
01216   {
01217     assert_len(n);
01218     return *std::next(begin(), n);
01219   }
01220 
01221   inline typename hook_chain::const_reference
01222       hook_chain::operator[](size_t n) const noexcept
01223   {
01224     assert_len(n);
01225     return *std::next(begin(), n);
01226   }

01228   inline typename hook_chain::reference hook_chain::at(size_t n)
01229   {
01230     verify_len(n);
01231     return *std::next(begin(), n);
01232   }

01235   {

01256   inline typename hook_chain::reference hook_chain::back() noexcept

01285   inline hook_chain::list_iterator hook_chain::append_hook(const hook& h,
01286                                                            transfer    trg)
01287   {
01288     
01289 assert(((void) "hook_chain::append_hook: to can't be the both flag" ,  trg != transfer::both ));
01290     auto [currentitr, enable_hook] =
01291         trg == transfer::enabled ? std::pair(std::prev(enabled.end()), true)
01292                                  : std::pair(std::prev(disabled.end()), false);
01293     push_back_impl(h.pdetour, h.origbuff, enable_hook);
01294     return ++currentitr;
01295   }

00782   template <typename T>
00783   template <typename itrbase>
00784   class helpers::regular_hook_map_base<T>::__const_itr : public itrbase
00785   {
00786   public:
00787     typedef std::pair<typename T::key_type, typename hook_chain::hook>
00788         value_type;
00789     typedef std::pair<const typename T::key_type&,
00790                       const typename hook_chain::hook&>
00791         reference;
00792 
00793     using typename itrbase::difference_type;
00794     using typename itrbase::iterator_category;
00795     using typename itrbase::pointer;
00796 
00797     __const_itr() noexcept {}
00798 
00799     __const_itr(itrbase itr) : itrbase(itr) {}
00800 
00801     reference operator*() const noexcept
00802     {
00803       auto ptr = itrbase::operator->();
00804       return std::make_pair(std::cref(ptr->first), std::cref(ptr->second));
00805     }
00806 
00807     __const_itr& operator++()
00808     {
00809       itrbase::operator++();
00810       return *this;
00811     }
00812 
00813     __const_itr operator++(int)
00814     {
00815       __const_itr tmp = *this;
00816       ++*this;
00817       return tmp;
00818     }
00819   };

00824   {

00826     typedef __const_itr<itrbase> base;
00827     typedef std::pair<const typename T::key_type&, typename hook_chain::hook&>

00832     using typename base::value_type;

00839     {
00840       auto ptr = __const_itr<itrbase>::operator->();
00841       return std::make_pair(std::cref(ptr->first), ptr->second);
00842     }

00847       return *this;
00848     }

00858   /*
00859    * ADAPTER HANDLING
00860    */
00861   namespace helpers
00862   {
00863     enum class adapter_type
00864     {
00865       NONE,
00866       REGULAR_UNIQUE_HOOK_MAP,           // eg. std::unordered_map
00867       REGULAR_MULTI_HOOK_MAP,            // eg. std::unordered_multimap
00868       CUSTOM_CONCURRENT_HOOK_MAP,        // eg. boost::concurrent_flat_map
00869       DEFAULT_CONCURRENT_HOOK_MAP,       // eg. std::unordered_multimap with
00870                                          // concurrent_mode = true
00871       DEFAULT_UNIQUE_CONCURRENT_HOOK_MAP // eg. std::unordered_map with
00872                                          // concurrent_mode = true
00873     };
00874 
00875     template <typename T>
00876     class bucket_api_base : public T
00877     {
00878     public:
00879       typedef T                                   base;
00880       typedef utils::first_template_param_of_t<T> adapted;
00881       typedef
00882           typename base::template __itr<typename adapted::const_local_iterator>
00883               local_iterator;
00884       typedef typename base::template __const_itr<
00885           typename adapted::const_local_iterator>
00886           const_local_iterator;
00887       using typename base::allocator_type;
00888       using typename base::chain_iterator;
00889       using typename base::const_chain_iterator;
00890       using typename base::const_hook_reference;
00891       using typename base::const_iterator;
00892       using typename base::const_list_iterator;
00893       using typename base::const_pointer;
00894       using typename base::const_reference;
00895       using typename base::const_reverse_list_iterator;
00896       using typename base::difference_type;
00897       using typename base::hasher;
00898       using typename base::hook;
00899       using typename base::hook_reference;
00900       using typename base::include;
00901       using typename base::iterator;
00902       using typename base::key_equal;
00903       using typename base::key_type;
00904       using typename base::list_iterator;
00905       using typename base::mapped_type;
00906       using typename base::pointer;
00907       using typename base::reference;
00908       using typename base::reverse_list_iterator;
00909       using typename base::size_type;
00910       using typename base::value_type;
00911       using transfer = typename base::transfer;
00912 
00913       using base::base;
00914 
00915       using base::begin;
00916       using base::cbegin;
00917       using base::cend;
00918       using base::end;
00919 
00920       local_iterator begin(size_type n)
00921       {
00922         return static_cast<local_iterator>(adapted::begin(n));
00923       }
00924 
00925       const_local_iterator begin(size_type n) const
00926       {
00927         return static_cast<const_local_iterator>(adapted::begin(n));
00928       }
00929 
00930       const_local_iterator cbegin(size_type n) const
00931       {
00932         return static_cast<const_local_iterator>(adapted::begin(n));
00933       }
00934 
00935       local_iterator end(size_type n)
00936       {
00937         return static_cast<local_iterator>(adapted::end(n));
00938       }
00939 
00940       const_local_iterator end(size_type n) const
00941       {
00942         return static_cast<const_local_iterator>(adapted::end(n));
00943       }
00944 
00945       const_local_iterator cend(size_type n) const
00946       {
00947         return static_cast<const_local_iterator>(adapted::end(n));
00948       }
00949 
00950       using base::bucket;
00951       using base::bucket_size;
00952       using base::max_bucket_count;
00953     };
00954 
00955     template <typename T,
00956               bool =
00957                   utils::closed_addressing<utils::first_template_param_of_t<T>>>
00958     struct add_bucket_api
00959     {
00960       typedef T type;
00961     };
00962 
00963     template <typename T>
00964     struct add_bucket_api<T, true>
00965     {
00966       typedef bucket_api_base<T> type;
00967     };
00968 
00969     template <typename T>
00970     using add_bucket_api_t = typename add_bucket_api<T>::type;
00971 
00972     template <typename T, adapter_type type = adapter_type::NONE>
00973     struct determine_adapter_impl
00974     {
00975       static_assert(utils::always_false<T>,
00976                     "couldn't find a suitable adapter for given hash map");
00977     };
00978 
00979     template <typename T>
00980     struct determine_adapter_impl<T, adapter_type::REGULAR_UNIQUE_HOOK_MAP>
00981     {
00982       typedef add_bucket_api_t<regular_unique_hook_map_base<T>> type;
00983     };
00984 
00985     template <typename T>
00986     struct determine_adapter_impl<T, adapter_type::REGULAR_MULTI_HOOK_MAP>
00987     {
00988       typedef add_bucket_api_t<regular_hook_map_base<T>> type;
00989     };
00990 
00991     template <typename T>
00992     struct determine_adapter_impl<T, adapter_type::CUSTOM_CONCURRENT_HOOK_MAP>
00993     {
00994       typedef custom_concurrent_hook_map_base<T> type;
00995     };
00996 
00997     template <typename T>
00998     struct determine_adapter_impl<T, adapter_type::DEFAULT_CONCURRENT_HOOK_MAP>
00999     {
01000       typedef default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T> type;
01001     };
01002 
01003     template <typename T>
01004     struct determine_adapter_impl<
01005         T, adapter_type::DEFAULT_UNIQUE_CONCURRENT_HOOK_MAP>
01006     {
01007       typedef default_unique_concurrent_hook_map_base<T> type;
01008     };
01009 
01010     template <typename T, bool concurrent_mode>
01011     struct determine_adapter
01012         : determine_adapter_impl<T, utils::regular_hash_map<T>
01013                                         ? adapter_type::REGULAR_UNIQUE_HOOK_MAP
01014                                     : utils::multi_hash_map<T>
01015                                         ? adapter_type::REGULAR_MULTI_HOOK_MAP
01016                                         : adapter_type::NONE>
01017     {
01018     };
01019 
01020     template <typename T>
01021     struct determine_adapter<T, true>
01022         : determine_adapter_impl<
01023               T, utils::regular_hash_map<T>
01024                      ? adapter_type::DEFAULT_UNIQUE_CONCURRENT_HOOK_MAP
01025                  : utils::multi_hash_map<T>
01026                      ? adapter_type::DEFAULT_CONCURRENT_HOOK_MAP
01027                  : utils::concurrent_hash_map<T>
01028                      ? adapter_type::CUSTOM_CONCURRENT_HOOK_MAP
01029                      : adapter_type::NONE>
01030     {
01031     };
01032   } // namespace helpers

01034   /*
01035    * TEMPLATE DEFINITIONS (ignore them)
01036    */
01037   template <typename T>
01038   template <size_t... k_indexes, size_t... d_indexes, size_t... o_indexes,
01039             typename... types>
01040   helpers::hook_map_base<T>::hook_map_base(std::byte* target,
01041                                            std::index_sequence<k_indexes...>,
01042                                            std::index_sequence<d_indexes...>,
01043                                            std::index_sequence<o_indexes...>,
01044                                            std::tuple<types...>&& args)
01045       : hook_chain(
01046             target,
01047             std::forward_as_tuple(
01048                 std::forward<
01049                     std::tuple_element_t<d_indexes, std::tuple<types...>>>(
01050                     std::get<d_indexes>(args)),
01051                 std::forward<
01052                     std::tuple_element_t<o_indexes, std::tuple<types...>>>(
01053                     std::get<o_indexes>(args)))...)
01054   {
01055     list_iterator itr = ebegin();
01056 
01057     (adapter::emplace(
01058          std::forward<std::tuple_element_t<k_indexes, std::tuple<types...>>>(
01059              std::get<k_indexes>(args)),
01060          std::ref(*(itr++))),
01061      ...);
01062   }
01063 
01064   template <typename T>
01065   template <typename key_t, typename detour_t, typename original_t,
01066             size_t... k_indexes, size_t... d_indexes, size_t... o_indexes,
01067             typename... types>
01068   auto helpers::hook_map_base<T>::insert_impl(
01069       transfer trg, std::index_sequence<k_indexes...>,
01070       std::index_sequence<d_indexes...>, std::index_sequence<o_indexes...>,
01071       std::tuple<key_t, detour_t, original_t, types...>&& args)
01072   {
01073     return insert_impl(
01074         trg, std::make_index_sequence<sizeof...(d_indexes)>(),
01075         std::tuple(std::forward_as_tuple(
01076                        std::forward<key_t>(std::get<0>(args)),
01077                        std::forward<std::tuple_element_t<
01078                            k_indexes,
01079                            std::tuple<key_t, detour_t, original_t, types...>>>(
01080                            std::get<k_indexes>(args))...),
01081                    std::forward_as_tuple(
01082                        std::forward<detour_t>(std::get<1>(args)),
01083                        std::forward<std::tuple_element_t<
01084                            d_indexes,
01085                            std::tuple<key_t, detour_t, original_t, types...>>>(
01086                            std::get<d_indexes>(args))...),
01087                    std::forward_as_tuple(
01088                        std::forward<original_t>(std::get<2>(args)),
01089                        std::forward<std::tuple_element_t<
01090                            o_indexes,
01091                            std::tuple<key_t, detour_t, original_t, types...>>>(
01092                            std::get<o_indexes>(args))...)));
01093   }
01094 
01095   template <typename T>
01096   template <typename kfirst, typename... keys, typename dfirst,
01097             typename... detours, typename ofirst, typename... originals,
01098             size_t... indexes>
01099   auto helpers::hook_map_base<T>::insert_impl(
01100       transfer trg, std::index_sequence<indexes...>,
01101       std::tuple<std::tuple<kfirst, keys...>, std::tuple<dfirst, detours...>,
01102                  std::tuple<ofirst, originals...>>&& args)
01103   {
01104     const bool enable_hook = trg == transfer::enabled;
01105 
01106     if constexpr (sizeof...(keys) == 0)
01107     {
01108       if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
01109       {
01110         base::push_back(std::forward<dfirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<1>(args))),
01111                         std::forward<ofirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<2>(args))),
01112                         enable_hook);
01113         try
01114         {
01115           return T::emplace(
01116               std::forward<kfirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<0>(args))),
01117               std::ref(enable_hook ? base::eback() : base::dback()));
01118         }
01119         catch (...)
01120         {
01121           base::pop_back(trg);
01122           throw;
01123         }
01124       }
01125       else if constexpr (utils::regular_hash_map<T>)
01126       {
01127         auto [result, status] =
01128             T::try_emplace(std::forward<kfirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<0>(args))),
01129                            base::empty_ref_wrap());
01130         if (!status)
01131           return std::pair(result, status);
01132         try
01133         {
01134           base::push_back(std::forward<dfirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<1>(args))),
01135                           std::forward<ofirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<2>(args))),
01136                           enable_hook);
01137         }
01138         catch (...)
01139         {
01140           T::erase(result);
01141           throw;
01142         }
01143         result->second = std::ref(enable_hook ? base::eback() : base::dback());
01144         return std::pair(result, status);
01145       }
01146       else
01147       {
01148         static_assert(utils::concurrent_hash_map<T>,
01149                       "not a concurrent map provided to insert as fallback");
01150         base::push_back(std::forward<dfirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<1>(args))),
01151                         std::forward<ofirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<2>(args))),
01152                         enable_hook);
01153         try
01154         {
01155           return T::try_emplace_or_cvisit(
01156               std::forward<kfirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<0>(args))),
01157               std::ref(enable_hook ? base::eback() : base::dback()),
01158               [&](const auto& ref) { base::pop_back(trg); });
01159         }
01160         catch (...)
01161         {
01162           base::pop_back(trg);
01163           throw;
01164         }
01165       }
01166     }
01167     else if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
01168     {
01169       list_iterator current =
01170           std::prev(enable_hook ? base::eend() : base::dend());
01171       base::append(
01172           trg,
01173           std::forward_as_tuple(
01174               std::forward<dfirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<1>(args))),
01175               std::forward<ofirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<2>(args)))),
01176           std::forward_as_tuple(
01177               std::forward<detours>(std::get<indexes + 1>(std::get<1>(args))),
01178               std::forward<originals>(
01179                   std::get<indexes + 1>(std::get<2>(args))))...);
01180       try
01181       {
01182         T::emplace(std::forward<kfirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<0>(args))),
01183                    std::ref(*(++current)));
01184         (T::emplace(
01185              std::forward<keys>(std::get<indexes + 1>(std::get<0>(args))),
01186              std::ref(*(++current))),
01187          ...);
01188       }
01189       catch (...)
01190       {
01191         base::erase(current, enable_hook ? base::eend() : base::dend());
01192         throw;
01193       }
01194       return size_t{ sizeof...(keys) + 1 };
01195     }
01196     else if constexpr (utils::regular_hash_map<T>)
01197     {
01198       utils::static_vector<typename base::hook, sizeof...(keys) + 1>
01199           tba_hooks{};
01200       utils::static_vector<typename T::iterator, sizeof...(keys) + 1> sources{};
01201       auto [result, status] =
01202           T::try_emplace(std::forward<kfirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<0>(args))),
01203                          base::empty_ref_wrap());
01204       if (status)
01205       {
01206         tba_hooks.push_back(base::hook_from(
01207             std::forward<dfirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<1>(args))),
01208             std::forward<ofirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<2>(args)))));
01209         sources.push_back(result);
01210       }
01211 
01212       try
01213       {
01214         ((std::tie(result, status) = T::try_emplace(
01215               std::forward<keys>(std::get<indexes + 1>(std::get<0>(args))),
01216               base::empty_ref_wrap()),
01217           status ? (tba_hooks.push_back(base::hook_from(
01218                         std::forward<detours>(
01219                             std::get<indexes + 1>(std::get<1>(args))),
01220                         std::forward<originals>(
01221                             std::get<indexes + 1>(std::get<2>(args))))),
01222                     sources.push_back(result), void())
01223                  : void()),
01224          ...);
01225 
01226         base::append_items(tba_hooks.begin(), tba_hooks.end(), trg);
01227       }
01228       catch (...)
01229       {
01230         for (auto itr : sources)
01231           T::erase(itr);
01232         throw;
01233       }
01234 
01235       list_iterator hitr = enable_hook ? base::eend() : base::dend();
01236       for (size_t i = sources.size(); i != 0; --i)
01237         sources[i - 1]->second = std::ref(*(--hitr));
01238       return sources.size();
01239     }
01240     else
01241     {
01242       base::push_back(std::forward<dfirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<1>(args))),
01243                       std::forward<ofirst>(std::get<0>(std::get<2>(args))),
01244                       enable_hook);
01245       bool   result = handle_emplacement<0, kfirst>(enable_hook, args);
01246       size_t count  = 0;
01247 
01248       if (!result)
01249         base::pop_back(trg);
01250       else
01251         ++count;
01252 
01253       ((base::push_back(
01254             std::forward<detours>(std::get<indexes + 1>(std::get<1>(args))),
01255             std::forward<originals>(std::get<indexes + 1>(std::get<2>(args))),
01256             enable_hook),
01257         result = handle_emplacement<indexes + 1, keys>(enable_hook, args),
01258         !result ? base::pop_back(trg) : (++count, void())),
01259        ...);
01260       return count;
01261     }
01262   }
01263 
01264   template <typename T>
01265   template <size_t N, typename type, typename args_t>
01266   bool helpers::hook_map_base<T>::handle_emplacement(bool    enable_hook,
01267                                                      args_t& args)
01268   {
01269     try
01270     {
01271       return T::try_emplace(
01272           std::forward<type>(std::get<N>(std::get<0>(args))),
01273           std::ref(enable_hook ? base::eback() : base::dback()));
01274     }
01275     catch (...)
01276     {
01277       base::pop_back(static_cast<transfer>(enable_hook));
01278       throw;
01279     }
01280   }
01281

01283   helpers::hook_map_base<T>::hook_map_base(std::byte* target) : base(target)
01284   {
01285   }

01298                                            dtr&& detour, orig& original,
01299                                            types&&... rest)
01300       : hook_map_base(
01301             target,
01302             utils::make_index_sequence_with_step<sizeof...(types) + 3, 0, 3>(),
01303             utils::make_index_sequence_with_step<sizeof...(types) + 3, 1, 3>(),
01304             utils::make_index_sequence_with_step<sizeof...(types) + 3, 2, 3>(),
01305             std::forward_as_tuple(std::forward<key>(first_key),
01306                                   std::forward<dtr>(detour), original,
01307                                   std::forward<types>(rest)...))

01323   template <typename T>
01324   template <typename tuple, typename... types, typename>
01325   helpers::hook_map_base<T>::hook_map_base(std::byte* target, tuple&& first,
01326                                            types&&... rest)
01327       : hook_chain(
01328             target,
01329             std::forward_as_tuple(
01330                 std::forward<
01331                     std::tuple_element_t<1, utils::remove_cvref_t<tuple>>>(
01332                     std::get<1>(first)),
01333                 std::get<2>(first)),
01334             std::forward_as_tuple(
01335                 std::forward<
01336                     std::tuple_element_t<1, utils::remove_cvref_t<types>>>(
01337                     std::get<1>(rest)),
01338                 std::get<2>(rest))...)
01339   {
01340     list_iterator itr = base::ebegin();
01341     adapter::emplace(
01342         std::forward<std::tuple_element_t<0, utils::remove_cvref_t<tuple>>>(
01343             std::get<0>(first)),
01344         std::ref(*(itr++)));
01345     (adapter::emplace(
01346          std::forward<std::tuple_element_t<0, utils::remove_cvref_t<types>>>(
01347              std::get<0>(rest)),
01348          std::ref(*(itr++))),
01349      ...);
01350   }

01362   helpers::hook_map_base<T>::hook_map_base(const hook_map_base& other)
01363       : hook_chain(other.get_target())
01364   {
01365     for (const auto& [k, v] : static_cast<const adapter&>(other))
01366       adapter::emplace(k, *append_hook(v));
01367   }

01390 
01391   template <typename T>
01392   helpers::hook_map_base<T>&
01393       helpers::hook_map_base<T>::operator=(const hook_map_base& other)
01394   {
01395     if (this != &other)
01396     {
01397       disable_all();
01398       set_trampoline(other.get_trampoline());
01399 
01400       for (auto itr = adapter::begin(), enditr = adapter::end(); itr != enditr;)
01401       {
01402         if (other.adapter::count(itr->first))
01403           ++itr;
01404         else
01405           itr = adapter::erase(itr);
01406       }
01407 
01408       if (adapter::size() >= other.adapter::size())
01409       {
01410         chain_iterator itr = base::begin();
01411         for (auto& [k, otheritr] : static_cast<const adapter&>(other))
01412         {
01413           set_item(*itr, static_cast<const hook&>(otheritr));
01414           adapter::insert_or_assign(k, std::ref(*(itr++)));
01415         }
01416 
01417         base::erase(itr, base::end());
01418       }
01419       else
01420       {
01421         typename adapter::const_iterator otheritr = other.adapter::begin();
01422         for (list_iterator itr = base::dbegin(), itrend = base::dend();
01423              itr != itrend; ++itr)
01424         {
01425           set_item(*itr, otheritr->second);
01426           adapter::insert_or_assign(otheritr->first, std::ref(*(itr++)));
01427         }
01428 
01429         for (typename adapter::const_iterator otherend = other.adapter::end();
01430              otheritr != otherend; ++otheritr)
01431           adapter::insert_or_assign(otheritr->first,
01432                                     std::ref(*append_hook(otheritr->second)));
01433       }
01434     }
01435     return *this;
01436   }
01437 
01438   template <typename T>
01439   helpers::hook_map_base<T>&
01440       helpers::hook_map_base<T>::operator=(hook_map_base&& other) noexcept
01441   {
01442     if (&other != this)
01443     {
01444       hook_chain::operator=(std::move(other));
01445       adapter::operator=(std::move(other));
01446     }
01447     return *this;
01448   }

01479 
01480   template <typename T>
01481   void helpers::hook_map_base<T>::merge(hook_map_base& other)
01482   {
01483     for (auto itr = other.adapter::begin(), itrend = other.adapter::end();
01484          itr != itrend; ++itr)
01485     {
01486       if (adapter::count(itr->first))
01487         continue;
01488       auto [flag, newpos] = itr->second.get().is_enabled()
01489                                 ? std::pair(transfer::enabled, base::eend())
01490                                 : std::pair(transfer::disabled, base::dend());
01491       base::splice(newpos, other, itr->second.get().get_list_iterator(), flag);
01492       adapter::insert(*itr);
01493       other.adapter::erase(itr);
01494     }
01495   }
01496 
01497   template <typename T>
01498   bool helpers::hook_map_base<T>::operator==(
01499       const hook_map_base& other) const noexcept
01500   {
01501     return std::equal(adapter::begin(), adapter::end(), other.adapter::begin(),
01502                       other.adapter::end(),
01503                       [](const auto& left, const auto& right)
01504                       {
01505                         return std::tie(left.first, left.second.get()) ==
01506                                std::tie(right.first, right.second.get());
01507                       });
01508   }
01509

01511   bool helpers::hook_map_base<T>::operator!=(
01512       const hook_map_base& other) const noexcept
01513   {
01514     return !operator==(other);
01515   }

01517   template <typename T>
01518   template <typename K, typename dtr, typename orig, typename... types,
01519             typename>
01520   auto helpers::hook_map_base<T>::insert(transfer trg, K&& key, dtr&& detour,
01521                                          orig& original, types&&... rest)
01522   {
01523     return insert_impl(
01524         trg, utils::make_index_sequence_with_step<sizeof...(rest) + 3, 3, 3>(),
01525         utils::make_index_sequence_with_step<sizeof...(rest) + 3, 4, 3>(),
01526         utils::make_index_sequence_with_step<sizeof...(rest) + 3, 5, 3>(),
01527         std::forward_as_tuple(std::forward<K>(key), std::forward<dtr>(detour),
01528                               original, std::forward<types>(rest)...));
01529   }

01532   template <typename K, typename dtr, typename orig, typename... types,
01533             typename>
01534   auto helpers::hook_map_base<T>::insert(K&& key, dtr&& detour, orig& original,
01535                                          types&&... rest)
01536   {
01537     return insert(transfer::enabled, std::forward<K>(key),
01538                   std::forward<dtr>(detour), original,
01539                   std::forward<types>(rest)...);
01540   }
01541 
01542   template <typename T>
01543   template <typename tuple, typename... types, typename>
01544   auto helpers::hook_map_base<T>::insert(transfer trg, tuple&& first,
01545                                          types&&... rest)
01546   {
01547     return insert_impl(
01548         trg, std::make_index_sequence<sizeof...(rest)>(),
01549         std::tuple(
01550             std::forward_as_tuple(
01551                 std::forward<
01552                     std::tuple_element_t<0, utils::remove_cvref_t<tuple>>>(
01553                     std::get<0>(first)),
01554                 std::forward<
01555                     std::tuple_element_t<0, utils::remove_cvref_t<types>>>(
01556                     std::get<0>(rest))...),
01557             std::forward_as_tuple(
01558                 std::forward<
01559                     std::tuple_element_t<1, utils::remove_cvref_t<tuple>>>(
01560                     std::get<1>(first)),
01561                 std::forward<
01562                     std::tuple_element_t<1, utils::remove_cvref_t<types>>>(
01563                     std::get<1>(rest))...),
01564             std::forward_as_tuple(
01565                 std::forward<
01566                     std::tuple_element_t<2, utils::remove_cvref_t<tuple>>>(
01567                     std::get<2>(first)),
01568                 std::forward<
01569                     std::tuple_element_t<2, utils::remove_cvref_t<types>>>(
01570                     std::get<2>(rest))...)));
01571   }

01574   template <typename tuple, typename... types, typename>
01575   auto helpers::hook_map_base<T>::insert(tuple&& first, types&&... rest)
01576   {
01577     return insert(transfer::enabled, std::forward<tuple>(first),
01578                   std::forward<types>(rest)...);
01579   }

01581   template <typename T>
01582   typename helpers::regular_hook_map_base<T>::iterator
01583       helpers::regular_hook_map_base<T>::erase(const_iterator pos)
01584   {
01585     hook_chain::erase(pos->second.get().get_list_iterator());
01586     return T::erase(pos);
01587   }
01588 
01589   template <typename T>
01590   typename helpers::regular_hook_map_base<T>::iterator
01591       helpers::regular_hook_map_base<T>::erase(const_iterator first,
01592                                                const_iterator last)
01593   {
01594     while (first != last)
01595     {
01596       hook_chain::erase(first->second.get().get_list_iterator());
01597       first = T::erase(first);
01598     }
01599     return last;
01600   }
01601 
01602   template <typename T>
01603   template <typename K>
01604   typename helpers::regular_hook_map_base<T>::size_type
01605       helpers::regular_hook_map_base<T>::erase(const K& k)
01606   {
01607     if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
01608     {
01609       auto   range = T::equal_range(k);
01610       size_t count = 0;
01611       while (range.first != range.second)
01612       {
01613         hook_chain::erase(range.first->second.get().get_list_iterator());
01614         range.first = T::erase(range.first);
01615         ++count;
01616       }
01617       return count;
01618     }
01619     else
01620     {
01621       auto result = T::find(k);
01622       if (result == T::cend())
01623         return 0;
01624       hook_chain::erase(result->second.get().get_list_iterator());
01625       T::erase(result);
01626       return 1;
01627     }
01628   }
01629 
01630   template <typename T>
01631   template <typename K, typename dtr, typename orig, typename... types,
01632             typename>
01633   auto helpers::regular_hook_map_base<T>::insert(transfer trg, K&& key,
01634                                                  dtr&& detour, orig& original,
01635                                                  types&&... rest)
01636   {
01637     auto result =
01638         base::insert(trg, std::forward<K>(key), std::forward<dtr>(detour),
01639                      original, std::forward<types>(rest)...);
01640     if constexpr (sizeof...(rest) == 0)
01641       return static_cast<insert_ret_t>(result);
01642     else
01643       return result;
01644   }

01664                                std::forward<types>(rest)...);

01678 
01679   template <typename T>
01680   template <typename K1, typename K2>
01681   void helpers::regular_hook_map_base<T>::swap(const K1& left, const K2& right)
01682   {
01683     if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
01684     {
01685       auto range_left = T::equal_range(left);
01686       if (range_left.first == range_left.second)
01687         throw(std::out_of_range("hook_map: out of range swap left operand"));
01688       auto range_right = T::equal_range(right);
01689       if (range_right.first == range_right.second)
01690         throw(std::out_of_range("hook_map: out of range swap right operand"));
01691       hook_chain::swap(range_left.first->second.get().get_list_iterator(),
01692                        range_right.first->second.get().get_list_iterator());
01693 
01694       auto [trgitrleft, trgitrright] =
01695           std::pair(range_right.first->second.get().get_iterator(),
01696                     range_left.first->second.get().get_iterator());
01697 
01698       ++range_right.first;
01699       ++range_left.first;
01700 
01701       for (auto itr_right = range_right.first; itr_right != range_right.second;
01702            ++itr_right)
01703       {
01704         hook_chain::splice(++trgitrleft,
01705                            itr_right->second.get().get_list_iterator());
01706         trgitrleft = itr_right->second.get().get_iterator();
01707       }
01708 
01709       for (auto itr_left = range_left.first; itr_left != range_left.second;
01710            ++itr_left)
01711       {
01712         hook_chain::splice(++trgitrright,
01713                            itr_left->second.get().get_list_iterator());
01714         trgitrright = itr_left->second.get().get_iterator();
01715       }
01716     }
01717     else
01718       hook_chain::swap(T::at(left).get().get_list_iterator(),
01719                        T::at(right).get().get_list_iterator());
01720   }
01721 
01722   template <typename T>
01723   template <typename K1, typename K2>
01724   void helpers::regular_hook_map_base<T>::splice(const K1& newpos,
01725                                                  const K2& oldpos)
01726   {
01727     if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
01728     {
01729       auto range = T::equal_range(oldpos);
01730       if (range.first == range.second)
01731         throw(std::out_of_range("hook_map: out of range splice oldpos"));
01732       auto newpositr = T::find(newpos);
01733       if (newpositr == T::end())
01734         throw(std::out_of_range("hook_map: out of range splice newpos"));
01735 
01736       for (auto itr = range.first; itr != range.second; ++itr)
01737         hook_chain::splice(newpositr->second.get().get_iterator(),
01738                            itr->second.get().get_list_iterator());
01739     }
01740     else
01741     {
01742       auto [hnewpos, holdpos] = std::make_pair(T::at(newpos), T::at(oldpos));
01743       hook_chain::splice(hnewpos.get_iterator(), holdpos.get_list_iterator());
01744     }
01745   }

01814   template <typename T>
01815   helpers::concurrent_hook_map_base<T>&
01816       helpers::concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::operator=(
01817           const concurrent_hook_map_base& other)
01818   {
01819     if (this != &other)
01820     {
01821       std::shared_lock lock1{ other.map_lock };
01822       std::unique_lock lock2{ map_lock };
01823       base::operator=(other);
01824     }
01825     return *this;
01826   }

01832   {
01833     if (this != &other)
01834     {
01835       std::unique_lock lock1{ other.map_lock };
01836       std::unique_lock lock2{ map_lock };
01837       base::operator=(std::move(other));
01838     }
01839     return *this;
01840   }

02094   template <typename T>
02095   template <typename callable, typename K, typename dtr, typename orig,
02096             typename>
02097   bool helpers::custom_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::insert_or_visit(
02098       K&& k, dtr&& detour, orig& original, callable&& func, transfer to)
02099   {
02100     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02101     if (T::visit(k,
02102                  [&](auto& pair) {
02103                    return func(
02104                        std::make_pair(std::cref(pair.first), pair.second));
02105                  }))
02106       return false;
02107     list_iterator pos =
02108         to == transfer::enabled ? hook_chain::eend() : hook_chain::dend();
02109     hook& h = hook_chain::insert(pos, std::forward<dtr>(detour), original, to);
02110     return T::emplace(std::forward<K>(k), std::ref(h));
02111   }
02112 
02113   template <typename T>
02114   template <typename callable, typename K, typename dtr, typename orig,
02115             typename>
02116   bool helpers::custom_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::insert_or_cvisit(
02117       K&& k, dtr&& detour, orig& original, callable&& func, transfer to)
02118   {
02119     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02120     if (T::cvisit(k,
02121                   [&](const auto& pair)
02122                   {
02123                     return func(std::make_pair(std::cref(pair.first),
02124                                                std::cref(pair.second)));
02125                   }))
02126       return false;
02127     list_iterator pos =
02128         to == transfer::enabled ? hook_chain::eend() : hook_chain::dend();
02129     hook& h = hook_chain::insert(pos, std::forward<dtr>(detour), original, to);
02130     return T::emplace(std::forward<K>(k), std::ref(h));
02131   }
02132 
02133   template <typename T>
02134   template <typename K>
02135   void helpers::custom_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::splice(const K& newpos,
02136                                                            const K& oldpos)
02137   {
02138     hook*            phnew = nullptr;
02139     hook*            phold = nullptr;
02140     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02141     if (!T::visit(newpos, [&](auto& pair) { phnew = &pair.second.get(); }))
02142       throw(std::out_of_range("hook_map: out of range splice newpos"));
02143     if (!T::visit(oldpos, [&](auto& pair) { phold = &pair.second.get(); }))
02144       throw(std::out_of_range("hook_map: out of range splice oldpos"));
02145     hook_chain::splice(phnew->get_iterator(), phold->get_list_iterator());
02146   }

02148   template <typename T>
02149   template <typename K>
02150   typename helpers::custom_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::size_type
02151       helpers::custom_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::erase(const K& k)
02152   {
02153     return T::erase_if(k,
02154                        [&](auto& pair)
02155                        {
02156                          std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02157                          hook_chain::erase(
02158                              pair.second.get().get_list_iterator());
02159                          return true;
02160                        });
02161   }

02215   template <typename T>
02216   template <typename K, typename callable>
02217   size_t helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::visit(const K&   k,
02218                                                              callable&& func)
02219   {
02220     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02221 
02222     if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
02223     {
02224       auto   range   = T::equal_range(k);
02225       size_t counter = 0;
02226 
02227       for (auto itr = range.first; itr != range.second; ++itr, ++counter)
02228         func(std::make_pair(std::cref(itr->first), itr->second));
02229       return counter;
02230     }
02231     else
02232     {
02233       auto result = T::find(k);
02234       if (result == T::end())
02235         return 0;
02236 
02237       func(std::make_pair(std::cref(result->first), result->second));
02238       return 1;
02239     }
02240   }
02241 
02242   template <typename T>
02243   template <typename K, typename callable>
02244   size_t
02245       helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::visit(const K&   k,
02246                                                           callable&& func) const
02247   {
02248     std::shared_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02249 
02250     if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
02251     {
02252       auto   range   = T::equal_range(k);
02253       size_t counter = 0;
02254 
02255       for (auto itr = range.first; itr != range.second; ++itr, ++counter)
02256         func(std::make_pair(std::cref(itr->first), std::cref(itr->second)));
02257       return counter;
02258     }
02259     else
02260     {
02261       auto result = T::find(k);
02262       if (result == T::end())
02263         return 0;
02264 
02265       func(std::make_pair(std::cref(result->first), std::cref(result->second)));
02266       return 1;
02267     }
02268   }

02275     return visit(k, std::forward<callable>(func));

02309 
02310   template <typename T>
02311   template <typename K1, typename K2>
02312   void helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::splice(const K1& newpos,
02313                                                             const K2& oldpos)
02314   {
02315     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02316 
02317     if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
02318     {
02319       auto range = T::equal_range(oldpos);
02320       if (range.first == range.second)
02321         throw(std::out_of_range("hook_map: out of range splice oldpos"));
02322       auto newpositr = T::find(newpos);
02323       if (newpositr == T::end())
02324         throw(std::out_of_range("hook_map: out of range splice newpos"));
02325 
02326       for (auto itr = range.first; itr != range.second; ++itr)
02327         hook_chain::splice(newpositr->second.get().get_iterator(),
02328                            itr->second.get().get_list_iterator());
02329     }
02330     else
02331     {
02332       auto [hnewpos, holdpos] = std::make_pair(T::at(newpos), T::at(oldpos));
02333       hook_chain::splice(hnewpos.get_iterator(), holdpos.get_list_iterator());
02334     }
02335   }
02336 
02337   template <typename T>
02338   template <typename K1, typename K2>
02339   void helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::swap(const K1& left,
02340                                                           const K2& right)
02341   {
02342     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02343 
02344     if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
02345     {
02346       auto range_left = T::equal_range(left);
02347       if (range_left.first == range_left.second)
02348         throw(std::out_of_range("hook_map: out of range swap left operand"));
02349       auto range_right = T::equal_range(right);
02350       if (range_right.first == range_right.second)
02351         throw(std::out_of_range("hook_map: out of range swap right operand"));
02352       hook_chain::swap(range_left.first->second.get().get_list_iterator(),
02353                        range_right.first->second.get().get_list_iterator());
02354 
02355       auto [trgitrleft, trgitrright] =
02356           std::pair(range_right.first->second.get().get_iterator(),
02357                     range_left.first->second.get().get_iterator());
02358 
02359       ++range_right.first;
02360       ++range_left.first;
02361 
02362       for (auto itr_right = range_right.first; itr_right != range_right.second;
02363            ++itr_right)
02364       {
02365         hook_chain::splice(++trgitrleft,
02366                            itr_right->second.get().get_list_iterator());
02367         trgitrleft = itr_right->second.get().get_iterator();
02368       }
02369 
02370       for (auto itr_left = range_left.first; itr_left != range_left.second;
02371            ++itr_left)
02372       {
02373         hook_chain::splice(++trgitrright,
02374                            itr_left->second.get().get_list_iterator());
02375         trgitrright = itr_left->second.get().get_iterator();
02376       }
02377     }
02378     else
02379       hook_chain::swap(T::at(left).get().get_list_iterator(),
02380                        T::at(right).get().get_list_iterator());
02381   }
02382 
02383   template <typename T>
02384   template <typename K, typename dtr, typename orig, typename... types,
02385             typename>
02386   auto helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::insert(
02387       transfer trg, K&& key, dtr&& detour, orig& original, types&&... rest)
02388   {
02389     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02390     auto             result =
02391         base::insert(trg, std::forward<K>(key), std::forward<dtr>(detour),
02392                      original, std::forward<types>(rest)...);
02393 
02394     if constexpr (sizeof...(rest) == 0)
02395       return result.second;
02396     else
02397       return result;
02398   }

02404                                                             dtr&& detour,

02409                   std::forward<dtr>(detour), original,
02410                   std::forward<types>(rest)...);
02411   }

02413   template <typename T>
02414   template <typename tuple, typename... types, typename>
02415   auto helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::insert(transfer trg,
02416                                                             tuple&&  first,
02417                                                             types&&... rest)
02418   {
02419     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02420     auto             result = base::insert(trg, std::forward<tuple>(first),
02421                                            std::forward<types>(rest)...);
02422 
02423     if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
02424       return true;
02425     else if constexpr (sizeof...(types) == 0)
02426       return result.second;
02427     else
02428       return result;
02429   }

02432   template <typename tuple, typename... types, typename>

02437                   std::forward<types>(rest)...);

02439 
02440   template <typename T>
02441   template <typename K>
02442   typename helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::size_type
02443       helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::erase(const K& k)
02444   {
02445     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02446 
02447     if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
02448     {
02449       auto   range   = T::equal_range(k);
02450       size_t counter = 0;
02451 
02452       while (range.first != range.second)
02453       {
02454         hook_chain::erase(range.first->second.get().get_list_iterator());
02455         range.first = T::erase(range.first);
02456         ++counter;
02457       }
02458       return counter;
02459     }
02460     else
02461     {
02462       auto result = T::find(k);
02463       if (result != T::end())
02464       {
02465         hook_chain::erase(result->second.get().get_list_iterator());
02466         T::erase(result);
02467         return 1;
02468       }
02469       return 0;
02470     }
02471   }
02472 
02473   template <typename T>
02474   template <typename K, typename callable>
02475   typename helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::size_type
02476       helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::erase_if(const K&   k,
02477                                                              callable&& func)
02478   {
02479     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02480 
02481     if constexpr (utils::multi_hash_map<T>)
02482     {
02483       auto   range   = T::equal_range(k);
02484       size_t counter = 0;
02485 
02486       while (range.first != range.second)
02487       {
02488         if (!func(std::make_pair(std::cref(range.first->first),
02489                                  range.first->second)))
02490         {
02491           ++range.first;
02492           continue;
02493         }
02494 
02495         hook_chain::erase(range.first->second.get().get_list_iterator());
02496         range.first = T::erase(range.first);
02497         ++counter;
02498       }
02499       return counter;
02500     }
02501     else
02502     {
02503       auto result = T::find(k);
02504       if (result == T::end())
02505         return 0;
02506 
02507       hook_chain::erase(result->second.get().get_list_iterator());
02508       T::erase(result);
02509       return 1;
02510     }
02511   }
02512 
02513   template <typename T>
02514   template <typename callable>
02515   typename helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::size_type
02516       helpers::default_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::erase_if(callable&& func)
02517   {
02518     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02519 
02520     for (auto itr = T::begin(), itrend = T::end(); itr != itrend;)
02521     {
02522       if (!func(std::make_pair(std::cref(itr->first), itr->second)))
02523       {
02524         ++itr;
02525         continue;
02526       }
02527 
02528       hook_chain::erase(itr->second.get().get_list_iterator());
02529       itr = T::erase(itr);
02530     }
02531   }

02588   template <typename T>
02589   template <typename callable, typename K, typename dtr, typename orig,
02590             typename>
02591   bool helpers::default_unique_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::insert_or_visit(
02592       K&& k, dtr&& detour, orig& original, callable&& func, transfer to)
02593   {
02594     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02595     auto             result = T::find(k);
02596     if (result != T::end())
02597     {
02598       func(std::make_pair(std::cref(result->first), result->second));
02599       return false;
02600     }
02601 
02602     list_iterator pos =
02603         to == transfer::enabled ? hook_chain::eend() : hook_chain::dend();
02604     hook& h = hook_chain::insert(pos, std::forward<dtr>(detour), original, to);
02605     T::emplace(std::forward<K>(k), std::ref(h));
02606     return true;
02607   }
02608 
02609   template <typename T>
02610   template <typename callable, typename K, typename dtr, typename orig,
02611             typename>
02612   bool helpers::default_unique_concurrent_hook_map_base<T>::insert_or_cvisit(
02613       K&& k, dtr&& detour, orig& original, callable&& func, transfer to)
02614   {
02615     std::unique_lock lock{ base::map_lock };
02616     auto             result = T::find(k);
02617     if (result != T::end())
02618     {
02619       func(std::make_pair(std::cref(result->first), std::cref(result->second)));
02620       return false;
02621     }
02622 
02623     list_iterator pos =
02624         to == transfer::enabled ? hook_chain::eend() : hook_chain::dend();
02625     hook& h = hook_chain::insert(pos, std::forward<dtr>(detour), original, to);
02626     T::emplace(std::forward<K>(k), std::ref(h));
02627     return true;

00146     if (!(--map->ref_count) && map->adapted::empty())
00147       instance.erase(map->get_target());
00148   }
00149 
00150   inline typename hook_manager::handle hook_manager::operator[](std::byte* key)
00151   {
00152     std::shared_lock             lock{ manager_lock };
00153     managed_concurrent_hook_map& entry = at(key);
00154     ++entry.ref_count;
00155     return handle(&entry);
00156   }
00157 
00158   inline typename hook_manager::const_handle
00159       hook_manager::operator[](std::byte* key) const
00160   {
00161     std::shared_lock                   lock{ manager_lock };
00162     const managed_concurrent_hook_map& entry = at(key);
00163     ++entry.ref_count;
00164     return const_handle(&entry);
00165   }
00166 
00167   template <typename trg, typename>
00168   typename hook_manager::handle hook_manager::operator[](trg&& target)
00169   {
00170     return operator[](get_target_address(std::forward<trg>(target)));
00171   }
00172 
00173   template <typename trg, typename>
00174   typename hook_manager::const_handle
00175       hook_manager::operator[](trg&& target) const
00176   {
00177     return operator[](get_target_address(std::forward<trg>(target)));
00178   }
00179 
00180   template <typename K, typename dtr, typename orig, typename... types>
00181   void hook_manager::insert(std::byte* target, K&& key, dtr&& detour,
00182                             orig& original, types&&... rest)
00183   {
00184     std::unique_lock lock{ manager_lock };
00185     auto [itr, status] = base::try_emplace(target, target);
00186     itr->second.insert(std::forward<K>(key), std::forward<dtr>(detour),
00187                        original, std::forward<types>(rest)...);
00188   }
00189 
00190   template <typename K>
00191   void hook_manager::erase(std::byte* target, const K& key)
00192   {
00193     typedef typename managed_concurrent_hook_map::adapted adapted;
00194 
00195     std::unique_lock lock{ manager_lock };
00196     auto             itr = base::find(target);
00197     if (itr == base::end())
00198       return;
00199     itr->second.erase(key);
00200     if (!itr->second.ref_count.load() && itr->second.adapted::empty())
00201       base::erase(target);
00202   }
00203 
00204   template <typename K>
00205   void hook_manager::enable(std::byte* target, const K& key)
00206   {
00207     std::shared_lock lock{ manager_lock };
00208     auto             itr = base::find(target);
00209     if (itr == base::end())
00210       return;
00211     itr->second.visit(key, [](auto pair) { pair.second.enable(); });
00212   }
00213 
00214   template <typename K>
00215   void hook_manager::disable(std::byte* target, const K& key)
00216   {
00217     std::shared_lock lock{ manager_lock };
00218     auto             itr = base::find(target);
00219     if (itr == base::end())
00220       return;
00221     itr->second.visit(key, [](auto pair) { pair.second.disable(); });
00222   }

00253         } -> std::same_as<bool>;
00254         {
00255           instance != instance
00256         } -> std::same_as<bool>;
00257         instance.swap(instance);
00258       };
